  17... # Drain
  18... REGION NUM=3 ix.l=26 ix.h=41 iy.l=10 iy.h=41 silicon

  25... REGION NUM=7 ix.l=26 ix.h=41 iy.l=41 iy.h=46 oxide

  26... ELECT NUM=1 x.min=0 x.max=0.05 y.min=0.07 y.max=0.07

  30... dop region=1 unif conc=5e+16 p.type
  31... dop region=2 unif conc=2e+20 n.type
  32... dop region=3 unif conc=2e+20 n.type
  33... dop region=4 unif conc=1e+18 p.type
  34... plot.3d doping outfile=pdr3400.doping

  36... $ Material specification

    ... + MUn=1400 VSATn=1.03e+07 En.Mu=2 IIN.MU=55.6,9.9e16,0.66,0.84,3.47e20
